        Our APIs make it easy to bring data from your app into Mailchimp, so you can manage your audience, trigger event-based emails, and more.    </p>
</li>
                    <li class="globalNav__navSectionL3">
        <ul>
                    <li data-context-metadata="{&quot;itemIndex&quot;:1,&quot;navPanel&quot;:null}">

    <p class="gn__descriptionCopy" id="l3description-3PM6QQwnXyVZG5JzzUxBUi">Use custom data from your app to power timely, relevant marketing campaigns.</p>
